function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 347') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.347!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// File added: dev/test/index.html
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('dev/test/index.html', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode(''));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('dev/test/index.html') && (sha1_file('dev/test/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/test/index.html');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/test/index.html');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/test/index.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/test/index.html', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('dev/test/index.html')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/test/index.html');
} else if (sha1_file('dev/test/index.html') != 'da39a3ee5e6b4b0d3255bfef95601890afd80709') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/test/index.html');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/test/index.html', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/test/index.html');
}

			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionSQLite3.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionSQLite3.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionSQLite3.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionSQLite3.class.php') !== '6b3972fd3ce5b572ee4aed72e32c4cf44fac6923') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/sqlite3/OIDplusDatabaseConnectionSQLite3.class.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 348\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 348') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
